    name VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,
    email VARCHAR(255) UNIQUE
);

    volunteer_id INT PRIMARY KEY,
    name VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,
    contact_number VARCHAR(15),
    organization_id INT,
    FOREIGN KEY (organization_id) REFERENCES nonprofit.organization(organization_id)
);</t><s>grant select, insert, update on nonprofit.donor to 'my_user';</s>

    donor_id INT,
    organization_id INT,
    amount DECIMAL(10, 2) NOT NULL,
    donation_date DATE,
    FOREIGN KEY (donor_id) REFERENCES nonprofit.donor(donor_id),
    FOREIGN KEY (organization_id) REFERENCES nonprofit.organization(organization_id)
);

CREATE TABLE nonprofit.donor (
    donor_id INT PRIMARY KEY,
    name VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,
    email VARCHAR(255) UNIQUE
);

CREATE TABLE nonprofit.volunteer (
    volunteer_id INT PRIMARY KEY,
    name VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,
    contact_number VARCHAR(15),
    organization_id INT,
    FOREIGN KEY (organization_id) REFERENCES nonprofit.organization(organization_id)
);</t><s>GRANT SELECT, INSERT, UPDATE ON nonprofit.donation TO 'my_user';</s>

    donation_id INT PRIMARY KEY,
    donor_id INT,
    organization_id INT,
    amount DECIMAL(10, 2) NOT NULL,
    donation_date DATE,

    FOREIGN KEY (organization_id) REFERENCES nonprofit.organization(organization_id)
);

CREATE TABLE nonprofit.project (id INT PRIMARY KEY, name VARCHAR, description TEXT, organization_id INT REFERENCES nonprofit.organization(id));

CREATE TABLE nonprofit.volunteer (id INT PRIMARY KEY, name VARCHAR, skillset TEXT, organization_id INT REFERENCES nonprofit.organization(id));</t><s>grant select, insert, update on nonprofit.project to project_manager;</s>
